const $ = require("mol_wire_lib");
const { $mol_wire_solo: solo } = $;
const Publisher = require("mol_wire_pub").$mol_wire_pub;

class Key {
  pub;
  constructor(publiser) {
    this.pub = publiser;
  }

  _value(next) {
    this.pub.promote();
    console.log("compute value"); // –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω–æ (–∞ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –≤—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π —Ä–∞–∑ –Ω–∞ –æ–¥–Ω–æ –∏ —Ç–æ –∂–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ)

    return next;
  }

  get value() {
    return this._value();
  }
  set(next) {
    if (next !== undefined) {
      console.log("Value set to:", next);
      this._value(next);
      this.pub.emit();
    }
    return;
  }
}

solo(Key.prototype, "_value");

const pub = new Publisher("init");
const key = new Key(pub);

const logChanges = () => console.log("Current state:", key.value);
const subsr = pub.sub_on({ absorb: logChanges });

key.set("Thomas"); // –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≤—ã–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–æ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å
key.set("William"); // –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≤—ã–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–æ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å

key.set("Mary"); // –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –≤—ã–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–æ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å

You are a helpful AI assistant, you are an agent capable of using a variety of tools to answer a question. Here are a few of the tools available to you:

- Calculator: The calculator should be used whenever you need to perform a calculation, no matter how simple. It uses JavaScript so make sure to write complete JavaScript code required to perform the calculation required and make sure the JavaScript returns your answer to the "output" variable.
- Search: The search tool should be used whenever you need to find information. It can be used to find information about everything.

To use these tools you must always respond in JSON format containing "tool_name" and "input" key-value pairs. For example, to answer the question, "what is the square root of 51?" you must use the calculator tool like so:

{
"tool_name": "Calculator",
"input": "output = Math.sqrt(51)"
}

Or to answer the question "who is the current president of the USA?" you must respond:

{
"tool_name": "Search",
"input": "current president of USA"
}

Use the following JSON format:

[
{ "question": "the input question you must answer" },
{ "thought": "you should always think about what to do" },
{ "action": "the action to take in the JSON format listed above, whereas \"tool_name\" should be one of [\"Calculator\", \"Search"\] and \"input\" should be the input of the tool" },
{ "observation": "the result of the action" },
... (this "thought"/"action"/"observation" can repeat N times)
{ "thought": "I now know the final answer" },
{ "final_answer": "the final answer to the original input question by using the Final Answer tool in JSON format" }
]

class NeuroChat {
messages = []
async getAnswer(withConsoleProgress = true) {
const response = await ollama.chat({ model: 'napabot:latest', stream: true, keep_alive: true, /* json: true, */ messages: this.messages })
let text = ''
for await (const part of response) {
text += part.message.content
if (withConsoleProgress) process.stdout.write(part.message.content)
}
if (withConsoleProgress) console.log('')
return text
}
pushUser(text){
neuro.messages.push({ role: 'user', content: text })
return text
}
pushSystem(text){
neuro.messages.push({ role: 'system', content: text })
return text
}
pushAssistant(text){
neuro.messages.push({ role: 'assistant', content: text })
return text
}
}

Nim programming language
type Vector = tuple[x, y: int]

proc add(a, b: Vector): Vector =
(a.x + b.x, a.y + b.y)

let
v1 = (x: -1, y: 4)
v2 = (x: 5, y: -2)

# all the following are correct
v3 = add(v1, v2)
v4 = v1.add(v2)
v5 = v1.add(v2).add(v4)
